is canceled.\n   105→// eventHandler() must be non-nil, and pollInterval must be greater than 0.\n   106→// eventHandler() is invoked whenever a change event is observed or pollInterval elapses.\n   107→// errorHandler() is invoked (if non-nil) whenever an error occurs initializing or watching the specified path.\n   108→//\n   109→// If path is a directory, only the directory and immediate children are watched.\n   110→//\n   111→// If path does not exist or cannot be watched, an error is passed to errorHandler() and eventHandler() is called at pollInterval.\n   112→//\n   113→// Multiple observed events may collapse to a single invocation of eventHandler().\n   114→//\n   115→// eventHandler() is invoked immediately after successful initialization of the filesystem watch,\n   116→// in case the path changed concurrent with calling WatchUntil().\n   117→func WatchUntil(ctx context.Context, pollInterval time.Duration, path string, eventHandler func(), errorHandler func(err The work queue pattern handles Remove/Rename events by re-establishing watches.\\n\\n4. **CA Bundle Reloading (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/dynamiccertificates/dynamic_cafile_content.go)**: Watches CA files using fsnotify, checks if CA changed with hasCAChanged() using bytes.Equal(), and atomically updates the CA bundle without disrupting client authentication.\\n\\n5. **Encryption Config Controller (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/encryptionconfig/controller/controller.go)**: Uses polling-based reload (PollUntilContextCancel with configurable interval) instead of fsnotify, checks file hash, and includes double-check TOCTOU prevention in processEncryptionConfig() before applying transformers.\\n\\n6. **Kubelet File Watcher (pkg/kubelet/config/file.go)**: Monitors pod manifest files via fsnotify with periodic polling fallback, converts filesystem events to pod updates, and handles backoff retry strategies.\\n\\n## Prometheus Hot-Reload Patterns\\n\\nPrometheus implements hot-reload through signal handlers, checksums, and coordinated subsystem reloads:\\n\\n1. **Configuration Reload Orchestration (cmd/prometheus/main.go)**: The reloadConfig() function is the central hot-reload orchestrator triggered by three mechanisms: SIGHUP signal handler, HTTP API endpoint, and automatic periodic polling. It uses configuration change detection before triggering subsystem reloads and records reload metrics (prometheus_config_last_reload_successful).\\n\\n2. **Config Diff Detection (config/reload.go)**: The GenerateChecksum() function implements lightweight change detection using SHA256 hashing of the config file plus all referenced external files (rule_files, scrape_config_files). This enables periodic polling without expensive config parsing.\\n\\n3. **Scrape Pool Reload (scrape/manager.go)**: The ApplyConfig() function atomically reloads scrape targets using reflect.DeepEqual() for config diff detection. It manages concurrent pool updates through a buffered triggerReload channel and performs atomic pool swaps in the scrapePools map with deferred cleanup of old pools.\\n\\n4. **Alertmanager Config Reload (notifier/manager.go)**: ApplyConfig() uses hash-based comparison for alertmanager sets and atomically swaps alert target sets while reusing compatible resources and deferring cleanup of obsolete configurations.\\n\\n5. **Discovery Manager Reload (discovery/manager.go)**: ApplyConfig() manages service discovery providers concurrently, canceling obsolete providers while registering new ones without interrupting existing target discovery.\\n\\n6. **File-Based Service Discovery (discovery/file/file.go)**: Implements event-driven discovery using fsnotify.Watcher with watchFiles() establishing watches on discovery files. Falls back to periodic ticker-based refresh on watcher failures and properly drains events during graceful shutdown.\\n\\n7. **Alert Rules Reload (rules/manager.go)**: The Update() function dynamically reloads alert rule files during config reload without process restart.\\n\\n8. **HTTP Reload Endpoint (web/web.go)**: The Reload() function exposes an HTTP API for triggering configuration reloads independent of signals, returning channels for async request handling.\\n\\n## Common Hot-Reload Patterns\\n\\nBoth Kubernetes and Prometheus share architectural patterns for zero-downtime configuration updates:\\n\\n- **File Watching**: fsnotify for event-driven monitoring with periodic polling fallback for reliability\\n- **Change Detection**: Byte-level equality checks (bytes.Equal) for files, hash comparison (SHA256) for periodic polling, and reflect.DeepEqual for structured config objects\\n- **Atomic Swaps**: atomic.Pointer and atomic.Value provide thread-safe configuration transitions without locks\\n- **Work Queues**: Rate-limited queues handle reload events with backoff retry logic\\n- **Concurrent Reload**: Independent subsystems reload concurrently via goroutines and buffered channels\\n- **Graceful Degradation**: Failed reloads don't affect current state; old resources are deferred cleanup\\n- **No Connection Drop**: Existing client/target connections are maintained across configuration updates\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

The work queue pattern handles Remove/Rename events by re-establishing watches.\\n\\n4. **CA Bundle Reloading (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/dynamiccertificates/dynamic_cafile_content.go)**: Watches CA files using fsnotify, checks if CA changed with hasCAChanged() using bytes.Equal(), and atomically updates the CA bundle without disrupting client authentication.\\n\\n5. **Encryption Config Controller (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/encryptionconfig/controller/controller.go)**: Uses polling-based reload (PollUntilContextCancel with configurable interval) instead of fsnotify, checks file hash, and includes double-check TOCTOU prevention in processEncryptionConfig() before applying transformers.\\n\\n6. **Kubelet File Watcher (pkg/kubelet/config/file.go)**: Monitors pod manifest files via fsnotify with periodic polling fallback, converts filesystem events to pod updates, and handles backoff retry strategies.\\n\\n## Prometheus Hot-Reload Patterns\\n\\nPrometheus implements hot-reload through signal handlers, checksums, and coordinated subsystem reloads:\\n\\n1. **Configuration Reload Orchestration (cmd/prometheus/main.go)**: The reloadConfig() function is the central hot-reload orchestrator triggered by three mechanisms: SIGHUP signal handler, HTTP API endpoint, and automatic periodic polling. It uses configuration change detection before triggering subsystem reloads and records reload metrics (prometheus_config_last_reload_successful).\\n\\n2. **Config Diff Detection (config/reload.go)**: The GenerateChecksum() function implements lightweight change detection using SHA256 hashing of the config file plus all referenced external files (rule_files, scrape_config_files). This enables periodic polling without expensive config parsing.\\n\\n3. **Scrape Pool Reload (scrape/manager.go)**: The ApplyConfig() function atomically reloads scrape targets using reflect.DeepEqual() for config diff detection. It manages concurrent pool updates through a buffered triggerReload channel and performs atomic pool swaps in the scrapePools map with deferred cleanup of old pools.\\n\\n4. **Alertmanager Config Reload (notifier/manager.go)**: ApplyConfig() uses hash-based comparison for alertmanager sets and atomically swaps alert target sets while reusing compatible resources and deferring cleanup of obsolete configurations.\\n\\n5. **Discovery Manager Reload (discovery/manager.go)**: ApplyConfig() manages service discovery providers concurrently, canceling obsolete providers while registering new ones without interrupting existing target discovery.\\n\\n6. **File-Based Service Discovery (discovery/file/file.go)**: Implements event-driven discovery using fsnotify.Watcher with watchFiles() establishing watches on discovery files. Falls back to periodic ticker-based refresh on watcher failures and properly drains events during graceful shutdown.\\n\\n7. **Alert Rules Reload (rules/manager.go)**: The Update() function dynamically reloads alert rule files during config reload without process restart.\\n\\n8. **HTTP Reload Endpoint (web/web.go)**: The Reload() function exposes an HTTP API for triggering configuration reloads independent of signals, returning channels for async request handling.\\n\\n## Common Hot-Reload Patterns\\n\\nBoth Kubernetes and Prometheus share architectural patterns for zero-downtime configuration updates:\\n\\n- **File Watching**: fsnotify for event-driven monitoring with periodic polling fallback for reliability\\n- **Change Detection**: Byte-level equality checks (bytes.Equal) for files, hash comparison (SHA256) for periodic polling, and reflect.DeepEqual for structured config objects\\n- **Atomic Swaps**: atomic.Pointer and atomic.Value provide thread-safe configuration transitions without locks\\n- **Work Queues**: Rate-limited queues handle reload events with backoff retry logic\\n- **Concurrent Reload**: Independent subsystems reload concurrently via goroutines and buffered channels\\n- **Graceful Degradation**: Failed reloads don't affect current state; old resources are deferred cleanup\\n- **No Connection Drop**: Existing client/target connections are maintained across configuration updates\\n\"\n}\n","numLines":176,"startLine":1,"totalLines":176}}}
